4/4/22:
	-Pre-session stuff:
		-Training:
			-Oh, 2 of our fellow Illuminated Solars have training Charms.
				-One has Tiger Warrior Training and it's sequel.
				-The other has the first Lore one.
				-TODO: plan some stuff for that?
					-Maybe with minimal detail, unless you want to figure out their Essence and
					 other stats.
			-Azada mentioned that the Sidereals had been manipulating fate to speed training during
			 the days of the Cult. Could such a thing be possible again?
			-The Emissary has been chipping in too, with crazy Bureaucracy charms.
				-She suggested the founding of a school, and I'm using my Training charms to create
				 a cadre of teachers for it, with a focus on "careers in Magictechnology!".
				-She seems pretty down, though, being listless, and mostly just going along with
				 whatever we want, taking little initiative herself.
				-Libak does seem to be trying to cheer her up.
		-Military, given the horde of monster-maggots on their way here:
			-Golden Blade and his henchmen saw to organizing militias and watch schedules, generally
			 prepping for a defense of the city's walls.
			-I spent my time on this front in the bowels of our Factory-Cathedrals, configuring them
			 for the production of arms.
				-We create a lot of:
					-Ashigaru Skirmish Armor (BoS I pg. 79)
					-Sentinel Defense Force Armor (BoS I pg. 81)
					-Perfected Boots (BoS I pg. 52)
					-Force-Projection Weapons (BoS I pg. 76)
					-Aegis-Inset Amulets (BoS 1 pg. 71)
					-Various mundane weaponry.
	-Those maggot monsters are on their way.
		-In their wake, they leave a trail of devestation and blight. They themselves consume any
		 plant or animal matter they can reach, and anything left quickly sickens.
		-We sent out some Ashigaru/Perfected Boots/Force-Projection Weapon equipped scouts, to get
		 an idea of the capabilities of these things.
		-They reported back that they explode satisfyingly when hit by the shock pikes, yielding no
		 ranged response from the beasts.
		-Well, sounds like hit and run tactics, along with raining death from above via the skyship,
		 should make short work of these beasts.
		-Golden Blade took Libak's war strider and set out with the skirmishers again, to harry the
		 horde, while the rest of us boarded the skyship, with Pip and Yflea manning the fire lances.
			-Blade and I each donned the Torcs, to let us communicate.
		-As we approached the maggots, though, those of us aboard the ship could see four more large
		 skyships, following the column of maggots.
			-One looks like a big pagoda.
			-The three others are large, octaganol platforms, with warstriders and soldiers standing
			 on them.
				-Most are smaller warstriders, though they're joined by a few large, red jade ones.
				-The soldiers are decked out much like our own, in Ashigaru armor.
			-Looking close, I could see an emblem I recognized as belonging to the 7th Legion. Lookshy.
		-Well, they're not likely to be _very_ friendly to Solars, but we also have a common problem.
		-As such, we descided to try to parley.
		-Through the use of signal flags, Libak disclaimed hostile intent, saying we're here to deal
		 with the maggots.
		-They signaled back that a parley can wait, but that we should deal with the maggots without
		 coming to blows.
		-We set to it, and soon nothing was left of the maggots but greasy, charred stains.
	-The left us with parleying with The 7th Legion. Their troops and warstriders began to assume a
	 parade formation at one end of a narrow valley.
		-We landed our airship and formed up at the other end of the valley, and Pip and Libak set
		 about forming a negotiating party.
			-Much to Pip's chagrin, we did not have a tea set in the skyship's minimal galley.
		-Two parties of soldiers marched forward from their group, while Libak and Pip walked
		 forward to meet them as the rest of us watched from a distance.
		-Pip and Libak returned, reporting an ultimatum: they wanted control of the Factory-Cathedrals
		 of Denandsor, and would take it from us or through us.
		-Well, none of us were keen to give up what's ours, and their position is not as sound as
		 they wish us to think.
			-They don't _want_ control of the Factory-Cathedrals, they _need_ it, or face
			 destruction by The Realm.
	-We opted to retreat, racing back to the city, by air and by magic boot.
		-As we left, we delivered a very literal parting shot, tying a message to an arrow and
		 shooting it land several yards in front of them. It said, "Ultimatum denied. If you want
		 the weapons, you either deal with Denandsor as a nation or burn your legions on trying to
		 take it."
		-As we raced back, they began boarding their airships again, and giving (thankfully slower
		 than us) pursuit.
		-Arriving back at the city, we saw to activating it's defenses.
			-Most of those are in the form of combat automata, but centuries-out-of-date programming
			 and similar accumluated cruft mean that's likely to lead to homicidal kill bots
			 attacking anyone they find in the city.
			-As such, I set about doing some debugging.
		-During the first hour Yflea and I spent working on that, the 7th Legion troops began
		 building and digging in, creating a fortified camp outside the city.
			-It was insufficient to encircle the city and lay seige to us, not that our supplies
			 are limited here. Might mean they're waiting on reinforcements.
			-We decided to send Silent Onyx out to sabotage their supplies, further weakening their
			 position here, and perhaps ruining the entire effort.
			-Soon we could see flames in the camp, and smoke rising from it. . .
			-He returned shortly after that, reporting a success in his mission.
				-He even said he'd stolen the hearthstones from several of the warstriders.
		-By the second hour of debugging, Yflea had returned with a group of my newly trained
		 scholars, to assist me in my work. I then finished clearing the instruction set in short
		 order, and taking full control over the city's defenses.
			-Mostly that's a magnitude 8, might 7 legion of automata, known as Brass Legionairres.
				-Their stats are in Roll20, under "AI NPCs", along with the stats for the rest of
				 this.
			-It also includes warstriders: common, scout, and noble types.
			-There's also a unit of hover copters, several units of cybernetic tanks, and hordes of
			 cybernetic dogs.
			-Many of the buildings also incorporate concealed lightening ballista, capable
			-Most impressive, though, is the function known as "The Dome", a shield that, when
			 activated, gives the whole city Adament Skin Technique, rendering it impenetrable to
			 harm, though also preventing anyone from leaving.
		-With that done, I utilized the PA system, announcing that, "The cities defenses are now
		 under our full control. The First Light's Dragon's circle should meet him in the control
		 room."
		-They soon did, and we arranged another party to parley with The 7th Legion.
		-As they walked out from the gates, a substantial chunk of that brass legion took to the
		 walls, saluting them as they passed. With Blade and I wearing the Torcs, I then brought
		 The Dome online as soon as they were outside the gate.
	-They met our party with one of their own, and negotiations began.
		-They clearly recognized the our new position of strength in these negotiations, though
		 there was the inevitable bit of sputtering.
		-In the end, we asked for:
			-Acknowledge our sovereignty.
			-Common defense against the Realm.
			-Denandsor will join The Confederation of Rivers in Nexus's place
			-They agree to forego allying with The Realm.
			-Raw materials in exchange for our Factory-Cathedral produced weapons and armor.
		-We also agreed to return their hearthstones to them, this being a red line for them, and
		 the stones being of little use to us ourselves.
		-They only requested one additional condition: that we show our loyalty to The Confederation
		 by immediately committing troops to the struggle against The Realm.
			-Blade has toops, we can see about training more, and we have _Solars_. _Insurgency_
			 trained Solars, who can raise more troops from the countryside, and turn them into
			 elite Tiger Warriors.
				-That last is also a hell of a propaganda win for us.
		-Both parties agreed to the terms.
		-With that, Denandsor then needs to choose a council member, to represent us on The
		 Confederacy's council in Marita.
			-Well, as I pointed out, we _do_ have an Emissary.
				-She's a known quantity, having led a member of The Confederacy for centuries, and
				 more than skilled for the purpose.
				-She and the others all agreed.
	-The Emissary went off to represent us at the council, leaving us to sort out the rule of the
	 city.
	-We also went about formalizing the rule of the city by our circle directly.
	-The other members of The Cult of the Illuminated were rather resistant to openly ruling, it
	 running very much contrary to everything they'd been taught.
		-Black Powder Jack, Nissen, and Jasara the Wise supported all us in that, though, and soon
		 the others fell in line.
	-We then had a season (3 months) of relative calm.
		-Shipments of materials from Lookshy indeed began arriving, with us reciprocating with the
		 promised arms.
			-Among those materials was a large shipment of Jade, and a small shipment of Orichalcum.
			-In fact, they indicated that they have some means of producing Orichalcum. . .
	-By the end of the season, The Realm was on the move, pushing into The Riverlands.
		-Their forces gather both North of Port Calin and South, near where Thorns _was_.
	-There was also, though, a barbarian horde gathering in the North of The Riverlands.
		-Combrised of bandits and other disaffected or dispossed people from the area, the horde
		 is pillaging everywhere they passed through.
	-One day, from the West, we saw again the Sword of Creation used, attacking somewhere to the
	 Northeast, in The Hundred Kingdoms.
	-Shortly thereafter, Infallible Messengers began to arrive, telling us of the arrival of Severus,
	 a dignitary from Lookshy, who will be arriving _in an hour_.
		-He appeared amidst a flurry of flower petals, in a row boat in one of Denandsor's ponds.
		-As we went out to greet him, he flashed, on his forehead, a caste mark, the sign of Venus.
		-Introducing himself as Yoshudo Severus, he said he had only recently Exalted.
		-He also bore with him a folded set of armor, red and ninja-style.
		-He said that he, representing Lookshy, wished to smuggle us into The Blessed Isle, to
		 disable The Sword of Creation.
			-Libak admitted we had some designs on just that, and I that we had access to certain
			 resources that might facilitate that.
		-"What say you?"
			-Golden Blade was first to respond, saying simply, "Tell me where to stab."
			-I said, "It would indeed be fascinating to finally see the inside of the of the
			 thing. . ."
			-The others hemmed and hawwed a bit, but went along with it.
		-"Excellent," he responded, "With this done, we will caste down The Empress, who's misrule
		 has continued for too look, and restore the rightful order."
		 "Restore the Shogunate?" I asked.
		 "Yes."
		-He then thrust forward his burden, saying, "This is The Crimson Armor of the Unseen
		 Assassin. It has the power to take you outside of Fate, hidden from any monitoring it."
		 "How did you come by such an artifact?" I asked, "Is some other faction, beyond Lookshy
		 backing you?
		 "I only know two others of my kind," he replied, "All of us operating out of Lookshy. I've
		 tried going to Heaven, but all of the gates are locked. . ."
		-We opted to consult with Azada on this, who enthusaistically suggested we do it, saying
		 that, "You should seize control of The Sword of Creation if possible, but disable it if
		 not. Either will deny it to the hand of our enemy."
		-Over the next several hours, we conferred with Severus about the details.
			-Lookshy is gearing up to invade The Realm, attacking The Imperial City directly, from
